Response to the Mandatory Requirements & Evaluation Criteria 

Mandatory Requirements

Our Team 

Jayme 

Relevant Experience

Availability and Mobilisation 

Our local team is ready for immediate mobilisation, followed closely by our global team and SME’s, all of which will be 100% available, ensuring a seamless and comprehensive approach. This phased mobilisation allows for rapid on-the-ground action while simultaneously leveraging the specialised knowledge and broader resources of our international network. This strategy ensures we can quickly adapt to evolving circumstances and reach into our global expertise of renewable energy while addressing critical needs and delivering innovation solutions from the outset while have personnel working around the clock, avoiding scope creep and budget blowouts. 

Understanding NSW and federal energy policy and energy infrastructure planning

Stakeholder Engagement 

Structured and Robust Communication and Stakeholder Engagement

Communication is the corner stone of any successful project, Egis has extensive experience in providing services across large-scale infrastructure projects, including those under Government procurement processes. We have successfully delivered multiple projects described in Section ABCD, and have a strong track record working in Integrated Product Teams (Working with the Technical Advisory and EnergyCo, engaging and communicating with multiple stakeholders, ensuring alignment with agreed deliverables and milestones between all parties. We will document how we will interact with and involve relevant stakeholders, either through supporting the development of a joint IPT communications plan or develop our own.

CVs 

Experience and Understanding

As a global leader in infrastructure consulting, engineering, and operation, Egis excels in hydrogen and wind farm projects. Egis and CBS are expert integrators of hydrogen projects and have been involved in hydrogen for over 10 years. Our expertise is designed to meet the challenges of the energy transition and the reduction of CO2 emissions, which has been used in PAU-lescar wastewater treatment plant project. Egis also has strong expertise in wind farm which were widely used for legal support, environmental studies, structural and geotechnical studies, integration to the grid and port engineering. Please refer to references and project example below. 

Risk Management

We understand that successful project delivery requires effective risk management, prompt issue resolution, and the identification of opportunities for continuous improvement. With our extensive experience in managing complex projects, including infrastructure and tolling systems across Australia and the Asia-Pacific region, we bring a risk-based approach (RBA) to every stage of the project, as we have on similar projects.

Our approach includes identifying and quantifying risks and issues across relevant disciplines and phases and include design, construction, testing, commissioning, operations, market, network, industrial relations, and asset ownership. We follow the AS/NZS 31000:2018 Risk Management framework, ensuring that management processes are structured and effective.

Risk and issue management includes managing risks inherent in delivering services and importantly, ensuring that the processes are in place to adequately solicit and manage to conclusion, the client’s and Contractors’ risks which could impact successful project delivery.

Project Timing and Scales

Timing: We employ an agile, time-optimised scheduling system, moving beyond traditional Gantt charts. This includes "just-in-time" resource allocation, micro-scheduling, and AI-driven predictive delay analysis, ensuring efficiency and proactive adjustments.

Scale: We provide scalable and modular solutions, rejecting the "one-size-fits-all" approach. Modular project frameworks, "plug-and-play" resource pools, cloud-based infrastructure, and digital twins allow for flexible adaptation to changing project needs and provide enhanced client visibility.

Relationship Management 

We foster collaborative, transparent partnerships, moving beyond standard meetings. "Relationship Pulse" surveys provide ongoing feedback, while online "Collaboration Hubs" enable real-time communication and collaboration. We will also run "Innovation Workshops", encouraging shared problem-solving, and client relationship scorecards offer clear performance visibility and identify areas for improvement.

Methodology

Approach 

Leveraging Global and Local SME

Egis will leverage Subject Matter Experts (SME) available both globally and locally. The Egis global reach enables us to tap into renewable energy SMEs, that have designed, delivered, commissioned similar technologies overseas. Their expertise will provide a deep understanding of challenges and issues with these RE technologies, together with potential impact they may have on communities and the environment.

Our 

 and coordinate 

Reporting

Culture of Sharing Knowledge

We understand that knowledge transfer and continuity are critical to the long-term success of renewable energy in Australia. Our team's deep experience working in this industry ensures a smooth integration of our advisory services with their operations. We implement structured succession planning, ensuring that key project knowledge is retained and passed on to the NSW Government team. Additionally, our approach includes mentoring and training programs designed to build capacity within TMR, preparing their workforce for future challenges and projects. By embedding knowledge transfer and planning for continuity, we guarantee that the NIS project will be supported by a highly capable, well-prepared team throughout its lifecycle.

Resourcing 

Maintaining a stable and skilled leadership team is paramount for the NIS project success. To address this, our team has nominated experienced senior members for key roles like PARROT, PARROT, and PARROT, ensuring they understand the project's scope and commitment. Our retention strategy focuses on creating a positive work environment through a 'culture-first' approach, offering competitive remuneration, providing ongoing professional development, and supporting relocation where needed. We're committed to unifying the team under a 'one team' ethos. Our track record, evidenced by low staff turnover on projects like PARROT, demonstrates our ability to attract and retain industry leaders. We've also established a robust succession plan with nominated back-up personnel, ensuring continuity in case of unforeseen circumstances. Formal mentoring programs will be implemented to develop junior engineers and graduates, fostering sustainable integration. Furthermore, comprehensive project documentation will be maintained, ensuring seamless knowledge transfer and continuity throughout the project.

Integration with clients 

Egis and CBS collaborate effectively with diverse stakeholders across numerous projects including PARROT, and QTMP. We understand that seamless integration and collaborative execution are critical to achieving optimal project outcomes, and we have refined our approach to ensure efficiency and transparency.

We are committed to adhering to the principles and requirements of ISO 44001, the international standard for collaborative business relationship management. This commitment underscores our dedication to fostering strong, mutually beneficial partnerships and ensuring effective collaboration within integrated program offices. We will implement and maintain a robust framework aligned with ISO 44001, ensuring consistent and effective collaborative practices across all projects.

We achieve successful integration, including seamless onsite collaboration, through a structured and proactive methodology, encompassing:

Dedicated Onsite Resources: We will provide dedicated resources to work onsite within your office, ensuring seamless integration and immediate responsiveness to project requirements. This allows for enhanced communication, rapid problem-solving stronger working relationships, and a deeper understanding of your organisation's culture and processes, fostering a collaborative workspace.

Integrated Project Management Systems: We leverage integrated project management systems to facilitate seamless data sharing, document control, and progress tracking. This ensures all stakeholders, including those working onsite, have access to real-time information, enabling collaborative problem-solving and informed decision-making.

Robust Communication Protocols: We implement comprehensive communication protocols, utilising a range of tools and platforms to ensure timely and accurate information dissemination. This includes regular progress meetings, detailed reporting, and proactive issue resolution. We understand that clear and consistent communication is paramount for maintaining transparency.

Response to the Mandatory Requirements & Evaluation Criteria 

Mandatory Requirements

Our Team 

Jayme 

Relevant Experience

Availability and Mobilisation 

Our local team is ready for immediate mobilisation, followed closely by our global team and SME’s, all of which will be 100% available, ensuring a seamless and comprehensive approach. This phased mobilisation allows for rapid on-the-ground action while simultaneously leveraging the specialised knowledge and broader resources of our international network. This strategy ensures we can quickly adapt to evolving circumstances and reach into our global expertise of renewable energy while addressing critical needs and delivering innovation solutions from the outset while have personnel working around the clock, avoiding scope creep and budget blowouts. 

Understanding NSW and federal energy policy and energy infrastructure planning

Stakeholder Engagement 

Structured and Robust Communication and Stakeholder Engagement

Communication is the corner stone of any successful project, Egis has extensive experience in providing services across large-scale infrastructure projects, including those under Government procurement processes. We have successfully delivered multiple projects described in Section ABCD, and have a strong track record working in Integrated Product Teams (Working with the Technical Advisory and EnergyCo, engaging and communicating with multiple stakeholders, ensuring alignment with agreed deliverables and milestones between all parties. We will document how we will interact with and involve relevant stakeholders, either through supporting the development of a joint IPT communications plan or develop our own.

CVs 

Experience and Understanding

As a global leader in infrastructure consulting, engineering, and operation, Egis excels in hydrogen and wind farm projects. Egis and CBS are expert integrators of hydrogen projects and have been involved in hydrogen for over 10 years. Our expertise is designed to meet the challenges of the energy transition and the reduction of CO2 emissions, which has been used in PAU-lescar wastewater treatment plant project. Egis also has strong expertise in wind farm which were widely used for legal support, environmental studies, structural and geotechnical studies, integration to the grid and port engineering. Please refer to references and project example below. 

Risk Management

We understand that successful project delivery requires effective risk management, prompt issue resolution, and the identification of opportunities for continuous improvement. With our extensive experience in managing complex projects, including infrastructure and tolling systems across Australia and the Asia-Pacific region, we bring a risk-based approach (RBA) to every stage of the project, as we have on similar projects.

Our approach includes identifying and quantifying risks and issues across relevant disciplines and phases and include design, construction, testing, commissioning, operations, market, network, industrial relations, and asset ownership. We follow the AS/NZS 31000:2018 Risk Management framework, ensuring that management processes are structured and effective.

Risk and issue management includes managing risks inherent in delivering services and importantly, ensuring that the processes are in place to adequately solicit and manage to conclusion, the client’s and Contractors’ risks which could impact successful project delivery.

Project Timing and Scales

Timing: We employ an agile, time-optimised scheduling system, moving beyond traditional Gantt charts. This includes "just-in-time" resource allocation, micro-scheduling, and AI-driven predictive delay analysis, ensuring efficiency and proactive adjustments.

Scale: We provide scalable and modular solutions, rejecting the "one-size-fits-all" approach. Modular project frameworks, "plug-and-play" resource pools, cloud-based infrastructure, and digital twins allow for flexible adaptation to changing project needs and provide enhanced client visibility.

Relationship Management 

We foster collaborative, transparent partnerships, moving beyond standard meetings. "Relationship Pulse" surveys provide ongoing feedback, while online "Collaboration Hubs" enable real-time communication and collaboration. We will also run "Innovation Workshops", encouraging shared problem-solving, and client relationship scorecards offer clear performance visibility and identify areas for improvement.

Methodology

Approach 

Leveraging Global and Local SME

Egis will leverage Subject Matter Experts (SME) available both globally and locally. The Egis global reach enables us to tap into renewable energy SMEs, that have designed, delivered, commissioned similar technologies overseas. Their expertise will provide a deep understanding of challenges and issues with these RE technologies, together with potential impact they may have on communities and the environment.

Our 

 and coordinate 

Reporting

Culture of Sharing Knowledge

We understand that knowledge transfer and continuity are critical to the long-term success of renewable energy in Australia. Our team's deep experience working in this industry ensures a smooth integration of our advisory services with their operations. We implement structured succession planning, ensuring that key project knowledge is retained and passed on to the NSW Government team. Additionally, our approach includes mentoring and training programs designed to build capacity within TMR, preparing their workforce for future challenges and projects. By embedding knowledge transfer and planning for continuity, we guarantee that the NIS project will be supported by a highly capable, well-prepared team throughout its lifecycle.

Resourcing 

Maintaining a stable and skilled leadership team is paramount for the NIS project success. To address this, our team has nominated experienced senior members for key roles like PARROT, PARROT, and PARROT, ensuring they understand the project's scope and commitment. Our retention strategy focuses on creating a positive work environment through a 'culture-first' approach, offering competitive remuneration, providing ongoing professional development, and supporting relocation where needed. We're committed to unifying the team under a 'one team' ethos. Our track record, evidenced by low staff turnover on projects like PARROT, demonstrates our ability to attract and retain industry leaders. We've also established a robust succession plan with nominated back-up personnel, ensuring continuity in case of unforeseen circumstances. Formal mentoring programs will be implemented to develop junior engineers and graduates, fostering sustainable integration. Furthermore, comprehensive project documentation will be maintained, ensuring seamless knowledge transfer and continuity throughout the project.

Integration with clients 

Egis and CBS collaborate effectively with diverse stakeholders across numerous projects including PARROT, and QTMP. We understand that seamless integration and collaborative execution are critical to achieving optimal project outcomes, and we have refined our approach to ensure efficiency and transparency.

We are committed to adhering to the principles and requirements of ISO 44001, the international standard for collaborative business relationship management. This commitment underscores our dedication to fostering strong, mutually beneficial partnerships and ensuring effective collaboration within integrated program offices. We will implement and maintain a robust framework aligned with ISO 44001, ensuring consistent and effective collaborative practices across all projects.

We achieve successful integration, including seamless onsite collaboration, through a structured and proactive methodology, encompassing:

Dedicated Onsite Resources: We will provide dedicated resources to work onsite within your office, ensuring seamless integration and immediate responsiveness to project requirements. This allows for enhanced communication, rapid problem-solving stronger working relationships, and a deeper understanding of your organisation's culture and processes, fostering a collaborative workspace.

Integrated Project Management Systems: We leverage integrated project management systems to facilitate seamless data sharing, document control, and progress tracking. This ensures all stakeholders, including those working onsite, have access to real-time information, enabling collaborative problem-solving and informed decision-making.

Robust Communication Protocols: We implement comprehensive communication protocols, utilising a range of tools and platforms to ensure timely and accurate information dissemination. This includes regular progress meetings, detailed reporting, and proactive issue resolution. We understand that clear and consistent communication is paramount for maintaining transparency.
